    2543                 :            :  * 'column' within 'row', deleting 'row', or completing an ongoing transaction.
    2544                 :            :  * If the returned value is needed for a long time, it is best to make a copy
    2545                 :            :  * of it with ovsdb_datum_clone(). */

    3759                 :            :  * type without updating the caller.)
    3760                 :            :  *
    3761                 :            :  * The caller must not modify or free the returned value.
    3762                 :            :  *
    3763                 :            :  * Various kinds of changes can invalidate the returned value: modifying
    3764                 :            :  * 'column' within 'row', deleting 'row', or completing an ongoing transaction.
    3765                 :            :  * If the returned value is needed for a long time, it is best to make a copy
    3766                 :            :  * of it with ovsdb_datum_clone(). */
